name:A‚Äçi‚Äçs‚Äçh‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçw‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äça‚Äçz‚Äçi
info:Standard Suite
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:19 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:Climbing Mount Tai during the Qingming Festival, I started booking hotels on the train from Jinan to Tai'an. I chose Tai'an Dongzun Ramada Plaza Hotel on Ctrip's hotel rankings. There were not many rooms left, so I booked an executive suite. When I checked in, the front desk directly upgraded it to a presidential suite.

I had only stayed in a presidential suite once before, and this time it was just right to experience it again. The room is on the top floor, the 9th floor. You don't need a card but a key. The entrance is the lobby, and then the mahjong room, next to the living room, the bedroom at the back, and the bathroom opposite. The room is long and narrow, irregular, and relatively large overall. It is spacious for two people. When Maru Azi was working, I played mahjong alone in the mahjong room and enjoyed it.

The room decoration is a bit old. There may not be many people staying in the presidential suite. Some facilities are not well maintained. The TV remote control has no power, and I can't find a hair dryer after taking a shower, but it does not cause inconvenience. The remote control on the Huawei mobile phone can turn on the TV. The rest of the facilities are the same as other room types. The quilt and pillow are very comfortable, and it is well received. I gave a lot of bottles of mineral water, but they were all ice dew, and the cost control was in place.

It was almost 12 o'clock when I checked in. I saw the view outside the window the next day. The view was nice.

I checked out the next day and stored my luggage. I came back from the mountain very late, so I stayed another night. This time I booked a standard room, but the experience was better. Because the view outside the 7th floor is very beautiful, there is a garden when you come out of the 7th floor, and you can go down along the garden to the hotel entrance.

I will stay here again next time I come to Mount Tai
